1. Exponential stability of data-driven nonlinear MPC based on input/output models

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16808v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：We consider nonlinear model predictive control (MPC) schemes using surrogate models in the optimization step based on input-output data only. We establish exponential stability for sufficiently long prediction horizons assuming exponential stabilizability and a proportional error bound. Moreover, we verify the imposed condition on the approximation using kernel interpolation and demonstrate the practical applicability to nonlinear systems with a numerical example.
  • 易漏细节梳理：

首先，为了优化步骤，基于输入-输出数据的代理模型被用于近似非线性系统。其次，假设系统在足够长的预测时间范围内具有指数稳定性。此外，为了验证近似条件，使用核插值方法来确保代理模型的准确性。因此，代理模型的建立依赖于输入-输出数据，而指数稳定性则依赖于预测时间范围的长度。最终，理论结果通过数值例子得到了支持，这些例子展示了代理模型在非线性系统中的实际应用。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • surrogate models are used in the optimization step based on input-output data only。
  • exponential stability is established for sufficiently long prediction horizons。
  • exponential stabilizability is assumed。
  • a proportional error bound is required。
  • kernel interpolation is used to verify the approximation condition。
  • numerical examples demonstrate practical applicability to nonlinear systems。
  • input-output data is the basis for surrogate models。
  • exponential stability depends on the prediction horizon length。
  • the condition on the approximation is verified using kernel interpolation。
  • theoretical results are supported by numerical examples。

2. Ultrafilter Extensions for Veltman Semantics

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16754v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：In this paper, we present a first-order frame condition for interpretability logic and show that the condition is not modally definable. Yet, the frame-condition holds both on ILM and on ILP frames and, hence, is of potential importance for the long-standing open problem about the interpretability logic of all reasonable arithmetical theories. In the light of the Goldblatt-Thomason Theorem, the modally inexpressible frame condition serves as motivation to develop ultrafilter extensions for inter pretability logic. We develop the necessary algebraic tools to define these ultrafilter extensions and prove the main properties about both the tools and the ultrafilter extensions.
  • 易漏细节梳理：

frame condition对于解释逻辑是不可模态定义的，这意味着在ILM和ILP框架上，它都成立。这一特性对所有合理算术理论的解释逻辑长期悬而未决的问题具有潜在重要性。Goldblatt-Thomason定理为开发超滤扩展提供了动机，而超滤扩展又需要相应的代数工具来定义。超滤扩展及其工具的主要性质已被证明，这些性质对于进一步研究解释逻辑具有重要意义。因此，frame condition的不可模态定义不仅在逻辑框架上具有普遍性，还为解决长期悬而未决的问题提供了新的途径。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • frame condition对于解释逻辑是不可模态定义的。
  • frame condition在ILM和ILP框架上都成立。
  • 模态不可表达的框架条件对所有合理算术理论的解释逻辑长期悬而未决的问题有潜在重要性。
  • Goldblatt-Thomason定理为开发超滤扩展提供了动机。
  • 超滤扩展需要相应的代数工具来定义。
  • 超滤扩展及其工具的主要性质已被证明。

3. How Do Language Models Acquire Character-Level Information?

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.05347v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Language models (LMs) have been reported to implicitly encode character-level information, despite not being explicitly provided during training. However, the mechanisms underlying this phenomenon remain largely unexplored. To reveal the mechanisms, we analyze how models acquire character-level knowledge by comparing LMs trained under controlled settings, such as specifying the pre-training dataset or tokenizer, with those trained under standard settings. We categorize the contributing factors into those independent of tokenization. Our analysis reveals that merge rules and orthographic constraints constitute primary factors arising from tokenization, whereas semantic associations of substrings and syntactic information function as key factors independent of tokenization.
  • 易漏细节梳理：

首先，字符级信息的隐式编码不依赖于训练时明确提供，这意味着语言模型能够通过学习文本中的模式和结构，自动获取字符级的信息。其次，分词方法会影响语言模型获取字符级信息的方式，不同的分词规则和拼写约束会引导模型以不同的方式处理字符级数据。此外，语义子字符串关联和句法信息是独立于分词的关键因素，这些信息帮助模型理解文本的深层含义和结构，从而更好地处理字符级数据。因此，通过控制训练设置，可以揭示语言模型是如何获取和利用这些字符级知识的机制。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • character-level信息的隐式编码不依赖于训练时明确提供。
  • merge规则和拼写约束是源于分词的主要因素。
  • 语义子字符串关联和句法信息是独立于分词的关键因素。
  • 控制训练设置可以揭示语言模型获取字符级知识的机制。
  • 分词方法会影响语言模型获取字符级信息的方式。
正文（点击展开）

4. General multi-Novikov algebras, multi-differential algebras and their free constructions

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16766v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Motivated by the recent development of noncommutative Novikov algebras and multi-Novikov algebras from the study of regularity structures of stochastic PDEs, this paper gives a general approach to study various multi-Novikov algebras and multi-differential algebras, with close connection with Poisson algebras. The construction of S. Gelfand of Novikov algebras from differential commutative algebras is generalized to this context. Free noncommuting multi-Novikov algebras are constructed from typed decorated rooted trees and from noncommuting multi-differential polynomials with populated conditions.

5. Robust $M$-Estimation of Scatter Matrices via Precision Structure Shrinkage

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.11099v2
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Maronna's and Tyler's $M$-estimators are among the most widely used robust estimators for scatter matrices. However, when the dimension of observations is relatively high, their performance can substantially deteriorate in certain situations, particularly in the presence of clustered outliers. To address this issue, we propose an estimator that shrinks the estimated precision matrix toward the identity matrix. We derive a sufficient condition for its existence, discuss its statistical interpretation, and establish upper and lower bounds for its additive finite sample breakdown point. Numerical experiments confirm the robustness of the proposed method.
  • 易漏细节梳理：

Maronna's和Tyler的$M$-估计量在高维设置下表现不佳，这主要是因为聚类异常值会显著降低$M$-估计量的性能。为了提高稳健性，可以将估计的精度矩阵向单位矩阵收缩，这种做法能够改善估计量的性能。研究中还推导出该提议估计量存在的充分条件，并对其统计解释进行了讨论。此外，还建立了提议估计量的分解点的上下界，这为衡量其对异常值的鲁棒性提供了指标。数值实验进一步证实了该方法的稳健性，表明它能够有效应对高维设置下的性能退化问题。从另一个角度看，提议的估计量可以被视为一种正则化形式，通过向单位矩阵收缩，它不仅提高了稳健性，还为异常值的鲁棒性提供了保障。因此，该方法不仅解决了高维设置下的性能退化问题，还通过分解点提供了衡量鲁棒性的指标，同时作为一种正则化形式，增强了估计量的稳健性。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • Maronna's and Tyler's $M$-estimators can perform poorly in high-dimensional settings.
  • Clustered outliers can significantly degrade the performance of $M$-estimators.
  • Shrinking the estimated precision matrix toward the identity matrix can improve robustness.
  • A sufficient condition for the existence of the proposed estimator is derived.
  • The statistical interpretation of the proposed estimator is discussed.
  • Upper and lower bounds for the breakdown point are established.
  • Numerical experiments confirm the robustness of the proposed method.
  • The proposed method addresses the issue of performance deterioration in high dimensions.
  • The breakdown point provides a measure of robustness against outliers.
  • The proposed estimator can be seen as a form of regularization.

6. Conservative Continuous-Time Treatment Optimization

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16789v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：We develop a conservative continuous-time stochastic control framework for treatment optimization from irregularly sampled patient trajectories. The unknown patient dynamics are modeled as a controlled stochastic differential equation with treatment as a continuous-time control. Naive model-based optimization can exploit model errors and propose out-of-support controls, so optimizing the estimated dynamics may not optimize the true dynamics. To limit extrapolation, we add a consistent signature-based MMD regularizer on path space that penalizes treatment plans whose induced trajectory distribution deviates from observed trajectories. The resulting objective minimizes a computable upper bound on the true cost. Experiments on benchmark datasets show improved robustness and performance compared to non-conservative baselines.
  • 易漏细节梳理：

模型误差可能导致提出超出支持范围的控制措施，这会增加实际操作中的风险和成本。为了解决这一问题，研究引入了一种保守方法，通过路径空间的一致签名MMD正则化来限制外推，从而确保提出的控制措施在实际操作中是可行的。这种方法的目标是通过计算可实现的上限来最小化真实成本，确保决策的稳健性。实验结果表明，与非保守的基线方法相比，该保守方法在鲁棒性和性能上表现更佳，进一步验证了其有效性。因此，通过这种正则化手段，可以有效减少因模型误差导致的不当控制措施，提高决策的可靠性。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • 模型误差可能导致提出超出支持范围的控制措施。
  • 保守方法通过路径空间的一致签名MMD正则化来限制外推。
  • 目标是通过计算可实现的上限来最小化真实成本。
  • 实验表明，与非保守基线相比，该方法具有更好的鲁棒性和性能。

7. Fish Audio S2 Technical Report

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08823v2
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：We introduce Fish Audio S2, an open-sourced text-to-speech system featuring multi-speaker, multi-turn generation, and, most importantly, instruction-following control via natural-language descriptions. To scale training, we develop a multi-stage training recipe together with a staged data pipeline covering video captioning and speech captioning, voice-quality assessment, and reward modeling. To push the frontier of open-source TTS, we release our model weights, fine-tuning code, and an SGLang-based inference engine. The inference engine is production-ready for streaming, achieving an RTF of 0.195 and a time-to-first-audio below 100 ms.Our code and weights are available on GitHub (https://github.com/fishaudio/fish-speech) and Hugging Face (https://huggingface.co/fishaudio/s2-pro). We highly encourage readers to visit https://fish.audio to try custom voices.
  • 易漏细节梳理：

Fish Audio S2 支持多说话人和多轮生成，通过自然语言描述实现指令跟随控制，这使得用户能够更灵活地与模型互动。为了进一步提升模型的性能和适应性，采用了多阶段训练方法，这种方法有助于扩大训练规模，提高模型的泛化能力。此外，发布的模型权重和微调代码是开放源代码的，这不仅方便了研究人员和开发者进行进一步的定制和优化，也促进了社区的共同进步。SGLang 基础的推理引擎适用于流媒体，确保了实时性的需求。实测结果显示，RTF 达到 0.195，时间到第一音频低于 100 毫秒，这表明模型具有出色的实时性能。读者可以访问 Fish Audio 网站尝试自定义声音，体验个性化的声音生成服务。代码和权重可在 GitHub 和 Hugging Face 上获取，为有兴趣的开发者提供了便捷的访问途径。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • Fish Audio S2 支持多说话人和多轮生成。
  • Fish Audio S2 通过自然语言描述实现指令跟随控制。
  • 多阶段训练方法有助于扩大训练规模。
  • 发布的模型权重和微调代码是开放源代码的。
  • SGLang 基础的推理引擎适用于流媒体。
  • RTF 达到 0.195，时间到第一音频低于 100 毫秒。
  • 代码和权重可在 GitHub 和 Hugging Face 上获取。
  • 鼓励读者访问 Fish Audio 网站尝试自定义声音。

8. An Extension of Major-Minor Mean Field Game Theory

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16534v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：This work extends the theory presented in Mean Field Games with a Dominating Player by Bensoussan, Chau and Yam on mean field games with a dominating player, to the case in which the utility and cost functions depend not only on the law of the states, but on the joint state--control law. We incorporate the conditional distribution of the state--control pair of the representative agent given the common noise of the dominating player. In addition, we generalize the role of the dominating player to include the direct impact of its controls $u_0$ on the dynamics and functionals of the system. The optimization problems are reformulated in terms of the conditional distribution of the state--control pair, the necessary optimality conditions are established via stochastic maximum principles, and a coupled SHJB--FP system of equations is obtained that synthesizes the equilibrium conditions. This framework provides a significant extension of the existing literature on MFG with a dominating player.
  • 易漏细节梳理：

首先，utility和成本函数不仅依赖于状态的分布，还依赖于状态-控制对的联合分布，这表明决策不仅基于当前状态，还考虑了可能采取的控制措施。其次，必须考虑支配玩家的共同噪声对代表代理的状态-控制对条件分布的影响，这意味着噪声不仅影响系统的动力学，还直接影响其功能。此外，支配玩家不仅影响系统的动力学，还直接影响其功能，这使得优化问题重新表述为状态-控制对的条件分布。因此，通过随机最大原则建立了必要的最优性条件，获得了一个耦合的SHJB-FP系统方程，综合了均衡条件。这不仅为现有的支配玩家的MFG理论提供了重要扩展，还使得理论更加全面和实用。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • utility和成本函数不仅依赖于状态的分布，还依赖于状态-控制对的联合分布。
  • 必须考虑支配玩家的共同噪声对代表代理的状态-控制对条件分布的影响。
  • 支配玩家不仅影响系统的动力学，还直接影响其功能。
  • 优化问题重新表述为状态-控制对的条件分布。
  • 通过随机最大原则建立了必要的最优性条件。
  • 获得了一个耦合的SHJB-FP系统方程，综合了均衡条件。
  • 这为现有的支配玩家的MFG理论提供了重要扩展。

9. Age-dependent random connection models with arc reciprocity: clustering and connectivity

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16824v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：We introduce a model for directed spatial networks. Starting from an age-based preferential attachment model in which all arcs point from younger to older vertices, we add \emph{reciprocal} connections whose probabilities depend on the age difference between their end-vertices. This yields a directed graph with reciprocal correlations, a power-law indegree distribution, and a tunable outdegree distribution. We consider two versions of the model: an infinite version embedded in $\mathbb{R}^d$, which can be constructed as a weight-dependent random connection model with a non-symmetric kernel, and a growing sequence of graphs on the unit torus that converges locally to the infinite model. Besides establishing the local limit result linking the two models, we investigate degree distributions, various directed clustering metrics, and directed percolation.
  • 易漏细节梳理：

在年龄基于偏好附接模型中，所有弧都指向较年轻的顶点，这反映了年龄对连接概率的影响。引入的模型中，互惠连接的概率依赖于端点顶点年龄差，这种机制使得概率不仅依赖于顶点的年龄，还依赖于它们之间的年龄差异。进一步地，该模型的无限版本可以嵌入在$\mathbb{R}^d$中，并构建为具有非对称核的权重依赖随机连接模型。这种模型的增长序列的图在单位环面上收敛到无限模型，从而使得研究度分布、各种有向聚类度量和有向渗流成为可能。此外，年龄依赖的随机连接模型能够产生幂律入度分布，而模型的出度分布则是可以调节的。因此，这些模型不仅能够模拟有向空间网络，还能通过局部极限结果将两个模型联系起来，从而提供了一种深入理解网络动态变化机制的工具。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • age-based preferential attachment模型中，所有弧都指向较年轻的顶点。
  • 引入的模型中，概率依赖于端点顶点年龄差的互惠连接。
  • 模型的无限版本嵌入在$\mathbb{R}^d$中，可以构建为具有非对称核的权重依赖随机连接模型。
  • 增长序列的图在单位环面上收敛到无限模型。
  • 研究了度分布、各种有向聚类度量和有向渗流。
  • 模型的局部极限结果将两个模型联系起来。
  • 年龄依赖的随机连接模型可以产生幂律入度分布。
  • 模型的出度分布是可以调节的。
  • 互惠连接的概率依赖于顶点年龄差。
  • 模型可以用于有向空间网络。

10. A Semantic Timbre Dataset for the Electric Guitar

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16682v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Understanding and manipulating timbre is central to audio synthesis, yet this remains under-explored in machine learning due to a lack of annotated datasets linking perceptual timbre dimensions to semantic descriptors. We present the Semantic Timbre Dataset, a curated collection of monophonic electric guitar sounds, each labeled with one of 19 semantic timbre descriptors and corresponding magnitudes. These descriptors were derived from a qualitative analysis of physical and virtual guitar effect units and applied systematically to clean guitar tones. The dataset bridges perceptual timbre and machine learning representations, supporting learning for timbre control and semantic audio generation. We validate the dataset by training a variational autoencoder (VAE) on its latent space and evaluating it using human perceptual judgments and descriptor classifiers. Results show that the VAE captures timbral structure and enables smooth interpolation across descriptors. We release the dataset, code, and evaluation protocols to support timbre-aware generative AI research.
  • 易漏细节梳理：

首先，精心策划的集合确保了数据集的质量和一致性，为后续处理奠定了基础。其次，通过使用语义描述符对数据进行标注，建立了感知与机器学习之间的桥梁，使得模型能够更好地理解数据的含义。此外，变分自编码器（VAE）的验证展示了数据集的有效性，证明了其在实际应用中的价值。因此，人类的感知判断确保了这些描述符的相关性，而平滑的描述符插值则进一步展示了VAE的能力。为了减少背景噪音，使用了干净的吉他音色。语义音色描述符提供了一个全面的框架，而通过训练潜空间则进一步提升了VAE的性能。最后，公开的代码和评估协议促进了研究的可重复性，使得其他研究者能够验证和改进这些模型。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • curated collection ensures quality and consistency in the dataset.
  • labeled with semantic descriptors provides a bridge between perception and machine learning.
  • variational autoencoder (VAE) validation demonstrates the dataset's effectiveness.
  • human perceptual judgments ensure the relevance of the descriptors.
  • smooth interpolation across descriptors showcases the VAE's capability.
  • clean guitar tones are used to avoid background noise.
  • semantic timbre descriptors offer a comprehensive framework.
  • latent space training enhances the VAE's performance.
  • code and evaluation protocols facilitate research replication.

11. Numerically stable variants of overrelaxation for operator Sinkhorn iteration

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12955v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：We consider accelerated versions of the operator Sinkhorn iteration (OSI) for solving scaling problems for completely positive maps. Based on the interpretation of OSI as alternating fixed point iteration, it has been recently proposed to achieve acceleration by means of nonlinear successive overrelaxation (SOR), e.g.~with respect to geodesics in Hilbert metric. The direct implementation of the proposed SOR algorithms, however, can be numerically unstable for ill-conditioned instances, limiting the achievable accuracy. Here we derive equivalent versions of OSI with SOR where, similar to the original OSI formulation, scalings are applied on the fly in order to take advantage of preconditioning effects. Numerical experiments confirm that this modification allows for numerically stable SOR-acceleration of OSI even in ill-conditioned cases.
  • 易漏细节梳理：

overrelaxation（过度松弛）可以加速 Sinkhorn 迭代过程，但直接实现可能在病态实例下不稳定。病态实例可能导致数值不稳定，从而限制了 SOR 加速的准确性。为了解决这一问题，可以通过动态应用缩放来实现数值稳定的 SOR 加速。具体而言，通过调整缩放因子，可以在保持加速效果的同时确保数值稳定性。数值实验验证了这种修改在病态情况下仍能保持数值稳定性，从而确保了算法的可靠性和准确性。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • overrelaxation 可以加速 Sinkhorn 迭代，但直接实现可能在病态实例下不稳定。
  • 病态实例可能导致数值不稳定，限制了 SOR 加速的准确性。
  • 通过动态应用缩放，可以实现数值稳定的 SOR 加速。
  • 数值实验验证了这种修改在病态情况下仍能保持数值稳定性。

12. Sub-cell Wave Reconstruction from Differentiated Riemann Variables

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16830v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：We introduce a postprocessing procedure that recovers sub-cell wave geometry from a standard one-dimensional Euler shock-capturing computation using differentiated Riemann variables (DRVs) -- characteristic derivatives that separate the three wave families into distinct localized spikes. Filtered DRV surrogates detect the waves, plateau sampling extracts the local states, and a pressure-wave-function Newton closure completes the geometry. The entire pipeline adds less than $0.25\%$ to the cost of a baseline WENO--5/HLLC solve. For Sod, a severe-expansion problem, and the LeBlanc shock tube, wave locations are recovered to within roundoff or $O(10^{-4})$ and the contact is sharpened to one cell width; a pattern-agnostic extension handles all four Riemann configurations with errors at the $10^{-6}$--$10^{-8}$ level. Direct comparison with MUSCL--THINC--BVD and WENO-Z--THINC--BVD shows that neither reproduces the combination of sharp contacts, small contact-window internal-energy error, and elimination of the LeBlanc positive overshoot achieved by the DRV reconstruction.
  • 易漏细节梳理：

filtered DRV surrogates能够准确检测波形，而plateau sampling则有助于精确提取局部状态。压力波函数Newton闭合则有效完成了几何构建，整个处理流程仅增加了极小的计算成本。通过这些方法，波的位置可以恢复到接近浮点误差或$O(10^{-4})$的精度，接触区域被锐化至一个网格单元宽度。此外，一种模式无关的扩展处理了所有四种Riemann配置，使得误差控制在$10^{-6}$至$10^{-8}$的水平。最终，DRV重建不仅实现了锐利的接触和小的内部能量误差，还消除了LeBlanc正向过冲现象。因此，这些方法共同确保了模型的高精度和高效性。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • filtered DRV surrogates can detect waves accurately.
  • plateau sampling helps extract local states precisely.
  • pressure-wave-function Newton closure completes the geometry effectively.
  • the entire pipeline adds minimal computational cost.
  • wave locations are recovered to within roundoff or $O(10^{-4})$.
  • contact is sharpened to one cell width.
  • a pattern-agnostic extension handles all four Riemann configurations.
  • errors are at the $10^{-6}$--$10^{-8}$ level.
  • DRV reconstruction achieves sharp contacts and small internal-energy error.
  • DRV reconstruction eliminates the LeBlanc positive overshoot.

13. OT-DETECT: Optimal transport-driven attack detection in cyber-physical systems

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16588v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：This article presents an optimal-transport (OT)-driven, distributionally robust attack detection algorithm, OT-DETECT, for cyber-physical systems (CPS) modeled as partially observed linear stochastic systems. The underlying detection problem is formulated as a minmax optimization problem using 1-Wasserstein ambiguity sets constructed from observer residuals under both the nominal (attack-free) and attacked regimes. We show that the minmax detection problem can be reduced to a finite-dimensional linear program for computing the worst-case distribution (WCD). Off-support residuals are handled via a kernel-smoothed score function that drives a CUSUM procedure for sequential detection. We also establish a non-asymptotic tail bound on the false-positive error of the CUSUM statistic under the nominal (attack-free) condition, under mild assumptions. Numerical illustrations are provided to evaluate the robustness properties of OT-DETECT.
  • 易漏细节梳理：

首先，minmax检测问题可以被减少为计算最坏情况分布的有限维线性规划问题，这为解决复杂检测问题提供了理论基础。其次，WCD（Wasserstein残差检测）的计算依赖于构造的1-Wasserstein不确定性集，该集基于观察器残差在正常和受攻击状态下的表现，从而确保了检测的准确性。此外，CUSUM程序用于顺序检测超出支持的残差，这种检测方法在实际应用中具有较高的灵敏度和可靠性。因此，非渐近尾部不等式适用于假阳性错误，尤其是在正常条件下，CUSUM统计的假阳性错误具有轻微假设的非渐近界，这进一步保证了检测的鲁棒性。最后，OT-DETECT算法的数值示例用于评估其鲁棒性，表明该算法适用于部分可观测的线性随机系统，从而在实际应用中具有广泛的应用前景。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • minmax检测问题可以被减少为计算最坏情况分布的有限维线性规划问题。
  • WCD的计算依赖于构造的1-Wasserstein不确定性集。
  • CUSUM程序用于顺序检测超出支持的残差。
  • 非渐近尾部不等式适用于假阳性错误。
  • OT-DETECT算法的数值示例用于评估其鲁棒性。
  • OT-DETECT适用于部分可观测的线性随机系统。
  • WCD的计算基于观察器残差在正常和受攻击状态下。
  • CUSUM统计的假阳性错误在正常条件下有轻微假设的非渐近界。

[2603.16588v1] OT-DETECT: Optimal transport-driven attack detection in cyber-physical systems Mathematics > Optimization and Control arXiv:2603.16588v1 (math) [Submitted on 17 Mar 2026] Title: OT-DETECT: Optimal transport-driven attack detection in cyber-physical systems Authors: Souvik Das , Siddhartha Ganguly View a PDF of the paper titled OT-DETECT: Optimal transport-driven attack detection in cyber-physical systems, by Souvik Das and Siddhartha Ganguly View PDF HTML (experimental) Abstract: This article presents an optimal-transport (OT)-driven, distributionally robust attack detection algorithm, OT-DETECT, for cyber-physical systems (CPS) modeled as partially observed linear stochastic systems. The underlying detection problem is formulated as a minmax optimization problem using 1-Wasserstein ambiguity sets constructed from observer residuals under both the nominal (attack-free) and attacked regimes. We show that the minmax detection problem can be reduced to a finite-dimensional linear program for computing the worst-case distribution (WCD). Off-support residuals are handled via a kernel-smoothed score function that drives a CUSUM procedure for sequential detection. We also establish a non-asymptotic tail bound on the false-positive error of the CUSUM statistic under the nominal (attack-free) condition, under mild assumptions. Numerical illustrations are provided to evaluate the robustness properties of OT-DETECT. 14. CABTO: Context-Aware Behavior Tree Grounding for Robot Manipulation

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16809v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Behavior Trees (BTs) offer a powerful paradigm for designing modular and reactive robot controllers. BT planning, an emerging field, provides theoretical guarantees for the automated generation of reliable BTs. However, BT planning typically assumes that a well-designed BT system is already grounded -- comprising high-level action models and low-level control policies -- which often requires extensive expert knowledge and manual effort. In this paper, we formalize the BT Grounding problem: the automated construction of a complete and consistent BT system. We analyze its complexity and introduce CABTO (Context-Aware Behavior Tree grOunding), the first framework to efficiently solve this challenge. CABTO leverages pre-trained Large Models (LMs) to heuristically search the space of action models and control policies, guided by contextual feedback from BT planners and environmental observations. Experiments spanning seven task sets across three distinct robotic manipulation scenarios demonstrate CABTO's effectiveness and efficiency in generating complete and consistent behavior tree systems.
  • 易漏细节梳理：

BT规划通常假设BT系统已经接地，这需要大量专家知识和手动努力，而BT接地问题则指出了自动构建完整且一致的BT系统的挑战。CABTO框架首次高效解决了这一问题，通过利用预训练的大模型来启发式搜索动作模型和控制策略的空间，从而克服了BT规划中依赖于高阶动作模型和低级控制策略的局限性。此外，BT规划通常由BT规划器的上下文反馈和环境观察引导，而CABTO则通过其高效的方法，在生成完整且一致的BT系统方面展现了显著的有效性。因此，CABTO不仅简化了BT系统的构建过程，还大幅提高了系统的质量和一致性。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • BT规划通常假设BT系统已经接地，这需要大量专家知识和手动努力。
  • BT接地问题是指自动构建完整且一致的BT系统的挑战。
  • CABTO框架首次高效解决了BT接地问题。
  • BT规划通常依赖于高阶动作模型和低级控制策略。
  • CABTO利用预训练的大模型来启发式搜索动作模型和控制策略的空间。
  • BT规划通常由BT规划器的上下文反馈和环境观察引导。
  • 实验展示了CABTO在生成完整且一致的BT系统方面的有效性。

15. Coherent RFRS groups

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16763v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：We prove that a finitely generated virtually RFRS group of cohomological dimension at most $2$ is coherent if and only if its second $L^{2}$-Betti number vanishes if and only if it is virtually free-by-cyclic. The non-vanishing of the second $L^{2}$-Betti number provides the first known global obstruction to coherence in any reasonably wide class of groups, allowing for proofs of incoherence without needing to exhibit explicit witnesses to incoherence. As applications of this result, we completely characterise coherence among two-dimensional Coxeter groups, confirming conjectures of Jankiewicz and Wise, and show that incoherence is generic in groups of nonpositive deficiency, confirming a conjecture of Wise. We also find that, among virtually compact special groups of virtual cohomological dimension two, coherence is algorithmically decidable and is a quasi-isometry, measure equivalence, and profinite invariant. In an appendix, Marco Linton applies one of the main results to prove that cubulated locally quasi-convex hyperbolic groups are virtually free-by-cyclic, solving problems of Abdenbi--Wise and Wise in the cubulated case.
  • 易漏细节梳理：

非零的第二 \(L^{2}\)-贝蒂数提供了一个全局障碍，阻止群的连贯性。具体而言，第二 \(L^{2}\)-贝蒂数的消失等价于该群几乎自由-循环。连贯性在几乎紧致特殊群中是可算法决定的，这些群的虚拟同调维数为2。连贯性是准同胚、测度等价和拟有限不变量。因此，立方体局部准凸双曲群几乎自由-循环。此外，连贯性在二维柯西特群中确认了Jankiewicz和Wise的猜想。另一方面，不连贯性在具有非正亏数的群中是普遍存在的，这确认了Wise的猜想。连贯的RFRS群是有限生成的几乎RFRS群，其同调维数不超过2。因此，连贯的RFRS群连贯性等价于其第二 \(L^{2}\)-贝蒂数消失，同时也等价于它几乎自由-循环。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • non-vanishing second $L^{2}$-Betti number provides a global obstruction to coherence.
  • second $L^{2}$-Betti number vanishing is equivalent to being virtually free-by-cyclic.
  • coherence is algorithmically decidable among virtually compact special groups of virtual cohomological dimension two.
  • coherence is a quasi-isometry, measure equivalence, and profinite invariant.
  • cubulated locally quasi-convex hyperbolic groups are virtually free-by-cyclic.
  • coherence among two-dimensional Coxeter groups confirms conjectures of Jankiewicz and Wise.
  • incoherence is generic in groups of nonpositive deficiency, confirming a conjecture of Wise.
  • coherent RFRS groups are finitely generated virtually RFRS groups of cohomological dimension at most 2.
  • coherent RFRS groups being coherent is equivalent to its second $L^{2}$-Betti number vanishing.
  • coherent RFRS groups being coherent is equivalent to it being virtually free-by-cyclic.

16. Training a force field for proteins and small molecules from scratch

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16770v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Force fields for molecular dynamics are usually developed manually, limiting their transferability and making systematic exploration of functional forms challenging. We developed a graph neural network that assigns all force field parameters for diverse molecules using continuous atom typing. The freely-available model, called Garnet, was trained on quantum mechanical, condensed phase and protein nuclear magnetic resonance data without the use of existing parameters. The resulting force field shows comparable performance to current force fields on small molecules, folded proteins, protein complexes and disordered proteins. It shows similar results to popular approaches for relative binding free energy predictions across a range of targets. Assessing different functional forms shows that the double exponential potential is a flexible and accurate alternative to the Lennard-Jones potential. Garnet provides a platform for automated, reproducible force field discovery that brings the benefits of machine learning to classical force fields.
  • 易漏细节梳理：

force fields 的开发通常需要手动进行，这限制了它们的可移植性。开发 force field 时，探索不同的功能形式具有挑战性。Garnet 模型作为一种自由提供的工具，通过量子力学、凝聚相和蛋白质核磁共振数据训练，未使用现有参数，为多种分子分配了所有 force field 参数。Garnet 模型在小分子、折叠蛋白质、蛋白质复合物和无序蛋白质上的表现与当前 force field 相当，且在相对结合自由能预测方面与流行方法具有相似的结果。评估不同的功能形式表明，双指数势是一种灵活且准确的替代 Lennard-Jones 势。因此，Garnet 提供了一个自动化的、可重复的 force field 发现平台，将机器学习的益处引入到经典 force field 中，显著提升了 force field 的开发效率和准确性。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • force fields 的开发通常需要手动进行，这限制了它们的可移植性。
  • 开发 force field 时，探索不同的功能形式具有挑战性。
  • Garnet 模型是自由提供的，用于为多种分子分配所有 force field 参数。
  • Garnet 模型是通过量子力学、凝聚相和蛋白质核磁共振数据训练的，未使用现有参数。
  • Garnet 模型在小分子、折叠蛋白质、蛋白质复合物和无序蛋白质上的表现与当前 force field 相当。
  • Garnet 模型在相对结合自由能预测方面与流行方法具有相似的结果。
  • 评估不同的功能形式表明，双指数势是一种灵活且准确的替代 Lennard-Jones 势。
  • Garnet 提供了一个自动化的、可重复的 force field 发现平台。
  • 机器学习的益处被引入到经典 force field 中。

17. SoMA: A Real-to-Sim Neural Simulator for Robotic Soft-body Manipulation

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.02402v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Simulating deformable objects under rich interactions remains a fundamental challenge for real-to-sim robot manipulation, with dynamics jointly driven by environmental effects and robot actions. Existing simulators rely on predefined physics or data-driven dynamics without robot-conditioned control, limiting accuracy, stability, and generalization. This paper presents SoMA, a 3D Gaussian Splat simulator for soft-body manipulation. SoMA couples deformable dynamics, environmental forces, and robot joint actions in a unified latent neural space for end-to-end real-to-sim simulation. Modeling interactions over learned Gaussian splats enables controllable, stable long-horizon manipulation and generalization beyond observed trajectories without predefined physical models. SoMA improves resimulation accuracy and generalization on real-world robot manipulation by 20%, enabling stable simulation of complex tasks such as long-horizon cloth folding.
  • 易漏细节梳理：

易漏但重要的end-to-end real-to-sim模拟要求模型同时考虑环境和机器人动作，这使得现有模拟器在准确性和泛化能力上存在局限。缺乏机器人条件控制是其中的关键问题，限制了现有模拟器的表现。为了解决这一问题，SoMA通过统一的潜在神经空间建模交互，显著提高了模拟的准确性。SoMA不仅能够进行可控和稳定的长期操作，还特别适用于未观察到的轨迹。因此，SoMA的改进使得复杂任务如长期布料折叠的模拟更加稳定。此外，SoMA通过学习的高斯斑点建模可变形动力学、环境力和机器人关节动作，进一步提升了模拟的精确度。最终，SoMA的改进使现实世界机器人操作的模拟重做准确性和泛化提高了20%。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • end-to-end real-to-sim simulation要求模型同时考虑环境和机器人动作。
  • 机器人条件控制的缺乏限制了现有模拟器的准确性和泛化能力。
  • SoMA通过统一的潜在神经空间建模交互，提高了模拟准确性。
  • SoMA允许在未观察到的轨迹上进行可控和稳定的长期操作。
  • SoMA的改进使复杂任务如长期布料折叠的模拟更加稳定。
  • 现有模拟器依赖预定义的物理模型或数据驱动的动力学。
  • SoMA通过学习的高斯斑点建模可变形动力学、环境力和机器人关节动作。
  • SoMA的改进使现实世界机器人操作的模拟重做准确性和泛化提高了20%。

Existing simulators rely on predefined physics or data-driven dynamics without robot-conditioned control, limiting accuracy, stability, and generalization. This paper presents SoMA, a 3D Gaussian Splat simulator for soft-body manipulation. SoMA couples deformable dynamics, environmental forces, and robot joint actions in a unified latent neural space for end-to-end real-to-sim simulation. 18. Learning Whole-Body Control for a Salamander Robot

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16683v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Amphibious legged robots inspired by salamanders are promising in applications in complex amphibious environments. However, despite the significant success of training controllers that achieve diverse locomotion behaviors in conventional quadrupedal robots, most salamander robots relied on central-pattern-generator (CPG)-based and model-based coordination strategies for locomotion control. Learning unified joint-level whole-body control that reliably transfers from simulation to highly articulated physical salamander robots remains relatively underexplored. In addition, few legged robots have tried learning-based controllers in amphibious environments. In this work, we employ Reinforcement Learning to map proprioceptive observations and commanded velocities to joint-level actions, allowing coordinated locomotor behaviors to emerge. To deploy these policies on hardware, we adopt a system-level real-to-sim matching and sim-to-real transfer strategy. The learned controller achieves stable and coordinated walking on both flat and uneven terrains in the real world. Beyond terrestrial locomotion, the framework enables transitions between walking and swimming in simulation, highlighting a
  • 易漏细节梳理：

学习四足机器人海龟机器人（salamander robots）的全身控制是一个被忽视的领域。研究人员利用强化学习将本体感受观察映射到关节级动作，从而实现稳定的行走，不仅在平坦地形上，也在不平坦地形上。尽管有少数四足机器人尝试在两栖环境中学习基于控制器，但海龟机器人主要依赖于中央模式发生器（CPG）和模型驱动的协调策略。全身控制从模拟环境转移到实际机器人中是一个挑战，而本体感受观察对于协调的运动行为至关重要。该研究工作集中在两栖四足机器人上，这些机器人模仿海龟的运动方式。为了实现硬件部署，研究采用了从现实到模拟（real-to-sim）和从模拟到现实（sim-to-real）的转移策略，使海龟机器人能够在行走和游泳之间进行转换。因此，通过强化学习和本体感受观察，海龟机器人能够实现全身控制，从而在两栖环境中表现出稳定的运动能力。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • learning whole-body control for salamander robots is underexplored.
  • reinforcement learning is used to map proprioceptive observations to joint-level actions.
  • the learned controller achieves stable walking on both flat and uneven terrains.
  • few legged robots have attempted learning-based controllers in amphibious environments.
  • the framework enables transitions between walking and swimming in simulation.
  • real-to-sim and sim-to-real transfer strategies are employed for hardware deployment.
  • salamander robots primarily use CPG-based and model-based coordination strategies.
  • whole-body control that transfers from simulation to physical robots is challenging.
  • proprioceptive observations are crucial for coordinated locomotor behaviors.
  • the work focuses on amphibious legged robots inspired by salamanders.

19. Two-loop Six-point Planar Massless Feynman Integrals to Higher $ε$ Orders

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16831v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：In this work, we calculate two-loop six-point planar massless Feynman integrals at higher orders in the dimensional regulator $ε$, corresponding to higher transcendental weights. In previous works, these integrals were calculated up to weight four for the purpose of two-loop gauge theory amplitudes. Using modern rational reconstruction methods, we identify the complete alphabet with $269$ letters relevant for the all-weight orders, derive the analytic canonical differential equation and obtain the symbols up to weight six. As a proof of concept, using a new method with Chebyshev pseudospectral transport, we show that the corresponding pure basis can be efficiently evaluated up to weight six, i.e., to $ \mathcal{O}(ε^2)$ in a physical scattering region. The results of this work can be applied to future three-loop amplitudes and provide new data for the formal study of symbols and cluster algebra.
  • 易漏细节梳理：

现代有理重构方法能够识别出269个字母，对应于所有权重的积分，这表明该方法具有较高的识别精度和广泛的应用范围。该工作展示了新的Chebyshev伪谱传输方法的有效性，这一方法不仅能够高效计算至六阶，还能够调节维数调节器ε，以计算至更高阶的积分，从而有助于理解更复杂的物理过程。与先前仅计算至四阶权重的工作相比，这一方法提供了更为精确的计算结果，为物理散射区域提供了精确计算。这些结果不仅为未来三环幅值的研究提供了新数据，也为符号和簇代数的正式研究提供了新数据，为未来高能物理实验提供了理论基础。因此，该研究不仅在理论上具有重要意义，还为实际应用提供了坚实的基础。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • 现代有理重构方法能识别出269个字母，对应于所有权重的积分。
  • 该工作展示了新的Chebyshev伪谱传输方法的有效性。
  • 结果可用于未来三环幅值的研究。
  • 纯基可以高效计算至六阶。
  • 这些结果为符号和簇代数的正式研究提供了新数据。
  • 积分计算至更高阶的维数调节器ε有助于理解更复杂的物理过程。
  • 先前的工作仅计算至四阶权重。
  • 该方法为物理散射区域提供了精确计算。
  • 该研究为未来高能物理实验提供了理论基础。

20. Regional Bias in Large Language Models

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.16349v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：This study investigates regional bias in large language models (LLMs), an emerging concern in AI fairness and global representation. We evaluate ten prominent LLMs: GPT-3.5, GPT-4o, Gemini 1.5 Flash, Gemini 1.0 Pro, Claude 3 Opus, Claude 3.5 Sonnet, Llama 3, Gemma 7B, Mistral 7B, and Vicuna-13B using a dataset of 100 carefully designed prompts that probe forced-choice decisions between regions under contextually neutral scenarios. We introduce FAZE, a prompt-based evaluation framework that measures regional bias on a 10-point scale, where higher scores indicate a stronger tendency to favor specific regions. Experimental results reveal substantial variation in bias levels across models, with GPT-3.5 exhibiting the highest bias score (9.5) and Claude 3.5 Sonnet scoring the lowest (2.5). These findings indicate that regional bias can meaningfully undermine the reliability, fairness, and inclusivity of LLM outputs in real-world, cross-cultural applications. This work contributes to AI fairness research by highlighting the importance of inclusive evaluation frameworks and systematic approaches for identifying and mitigating geographic biases in language models.
  • 易漏细节梳理：

FAZE框架通过10分制衡量区域偏见，分数越高表示对特定区域的偏好越强。实验结果显示，不同模型在区域偏见上的表现差异显著，其中GPT-3.5得分最高，表明其对特定区域的偏好最强；而Claude 3.5 Sonnet得分最低，表明其对特定区域的偏好最弱。区域偏见可能严重影响语言模型在实际应用中的可靠性和公平性，因此FAZE框架有助于识别和减轻语言模型中的地理偏见。不同模型在区域偏见上的表现差异可能反映出不同的训练数据集，而区域偏见可能因模型的不同而异，需要具体分析。此外，区域偏见可能因模型的训练数据和架构而异，甚至在不同文化背景下影响语言模型的输出。因此，评估语言模型的公平性时，区域偏见是一个重要方面。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • FAZE框架通过10分制衡量区域偏见，分数越高表示对特定区域的偏好越强。
  • 实验结果显示，不同模型在区域偏见上的表现差异显著。
  • GPT-3.5在区域偏见上得分最高，表明其对特定区域的偏好最强。
  • Claude 3.5 Sonnet在区域偏见上得分最低，表明其对特定区域的偏好最弱。
  • 区域偏见可能严重影响语言模型在实际应用中的可靠性和公平性。
  • FAZE框架有助于识别和减轻语言模型中的地理偏见。
  • 区域偏见是评估语言模型公平性的重要方面。
  • 不同模型在区域偏见上的表现差异可能反映出不同的训练数据集。
  • 区域偏见可能因模型的不同而异，需要具体分析。
  • 区域偏见可能因模型的训练数据和架构而异。
  • 区域偏见可能在不同文化背景下影响语言模型的输出。

21. pADAM: A Plug-and-Play All-in-One Diffusion Architecture for Multi-Physics Learning

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16757v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Generalizing across disparate physical laws remains a fundamental challenge for artificial intelligence in science. Existing deep-learning solvers are largely confined to single-equation settings, limiting transfer across physical regimes and inference tasks. Here we introduce pADAM, a unified generative framework that learns a shared probabilistic prior across heterogeneous partial differential equation families. Through a learned joint distribution of system states and, where applicable, physical parameters, pADAM supports forward prediction and inverse inference within a single architecture without retraining. Across benchmarks ranging from scalar diffusion to nonlinear Navier--Stokes equations, pADAM achieves accurate inference even under sparse observations. Combined with conformal prediction, it also provides reliable uncertainty quantification with coverage guarantees. In addition, pADAM performs probabilistic model selection from only two sparse snapshots, identifying governing laws through its learned generative representation. These results highlight the potential of generative multi-physics modeling for unified and uncertainty-aware scientific inference.
  • 易漏细节梳理：

pADAM 的应用不限于单一物理方程，而是适用于多种物理方程，这使得它在处理复杂系统时更具灵活性。pADAM 通过学习联合分布支持前向预测和逆向推理，从而能够从不同角度理解和解释物理现象。在稀疏观测的情况下，pADAM 仍能实现准确的推理，这表明它具有强大的适应性和鲁棒性。此外，pADAM 结合协性预测可以提供可靠且有覆盖保证的不确定性量化，进一步增强了其在不确定性感知科学推理中的能力。pADAM 还能够仅通过两个稀疏快照进行概率模型选择，这大大减少了数据需求，提高了效率。学习生成表示有助于pADAM 识别支配规律，从而更好地理解物理系统的本质。因此，pADAM 的结果突显了生成式多物理建模在统一和不确定性感知科学推理中的潜力，展示了其在现代科学中的广泛应用和重要性。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • pADAM 的应用不限于单一物理方程，而是适用于多种物理方程。
  • pADAM 通过学习联合分布支持前向预测和逆向推理。
  • pADAM 在稀疏观测下仍能实现准确的推理。
  • pADAM 结合协性预测可以提供可靠且有覆盖保证的不确定性量化。
  • pADAM 可以仅通过两个稀疏快照进行概率模型选择。
  • pADAM 的学习生成表示有助于识别支配规律。
  • pADAM 的结果突显了生成式多物理建模在统一和不确定性感知科学推理中的潜力。

22. Online Experiential Learning for Language Models

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16856v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：The prevailing paradigm for improving large language models relies on offline training with human annotations or simulated environments, leaving the rich experience accumulated during real-world deployment entirely unexploited. We propose Online Experiential Learning (OEL), a framework that enables language models to continuously improve from their own deployment experience. OEL operates in two stages: first, transferable experiential knowledge is extracted and accumulated from interaction trajectories collected on the user side; second, this knowledge is consolidated into model parameters via on-policy context distillation, requiring no access to the user-side environment. The two stages are iterated to form an online learning loop, where the improved model collects higher-quality trajectories that yield richer experiential knowledge for subsequent rounds. We evaluate OEL on text-based game environments across multiple model scales and both thinking and non-thinking variants. OEL achieves consistent improvements over successive iterations, enhancing both task accuracy and token efficiency while preserving out-of-distribution performance. Our analysis further shows that extracted e
  • 易漏细节梳理：

线下训练通常依赖于人工标注或模拟环境，但这些方法可能忽视了实际部署经验。因此，从用户侧收集的交互轨迹被用于提取可转移的经验知识。通过在线策略上下文蒸馏，知识被整合进模型参数，无需访问用户侧环境。改进后的模型能够收集更高质量的轨迹，从而为后续轮次提供更丰富的经验知识。在线增强学习（OEL）通过持续迭代实现一致改进，提升任务准确性和令牌效率。提取的经验知识比原始轨迹更为有效。在线策略的一致性对于有效学习至关重要。传统离线训练方法未能充分利用实际部署中的丰富经验。所提出的框架在文本游戏环境中进行评估，跨越多个模型规模，展示了其在线学习循环的优势。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • offline training with human annotations or simulated environments may overlook real-world deployment experience.
  • interaction trajectories collected on the user side are used to extract transferable experiential knowledge.
  • on-policy context distillation consolidates knowledge into model parameters without needing access to the user-side environment.
  • improved models collect higher-quality trajectories, leading to richer experiential knowledge for subsequent rounds.
  • OEL achieves consistent improvements over successive iterations, enhancing task accuracy and token efficiency.
  • extracted experiential knowledge is significantly more effective than raw trajectories.
  • on-policy consistency between the knowledge source and the policy model is crucial for effective learning.
  • rich experience from real-world deployment is unexploited in traditional offline training methods.
  • the proposed framework operates in an online learning loop, continuously improving the model.
  • text-based game environments are used to evaluate the proposed framework across multiple model scales.

[2603.16856v1] Online Experiential Learning for Language Models Computer Science > Computation and Language arXiv:2603.16856v1 (cs) [Submitted on 17 Mar 2026] Title: Online Experiential Learning for Language Models Authors: Tianzhu Ye , Li Dong , Qingxiu Dong , Xun Wu , Shaohan Huang , Furu Wei View a PDF of the paper titled Online Experiential Learning for Language Models, by Tianzhu Ye and 5 other authors View PDF HTML (experimental) Abstract: The prevailing paradigm for improving large language models relies on offline training with human annotations or simulated environments, leaving the rich experience accumulated during real-world deployment entirely unexploited. We propose Online Experiential Learning (OEL), a framework that enables language models to continuously improve from their own deployment experience. OEL operates in two stages: first, transferable experiential knowledge is extracted and accumulated from interaction trajectories collected on the user side; second, this knowledge is consolidated into model parameters via on-policy context distillation, requiring no access to the user-side environment. The two stages are iterated to form an online learning loop, where the improved model collects higher-quality trajectories that yield richer experiential knowledge for subsequent rounds. We evaluate OEL on text-based game environments across multiple model scales and both thinking and non-thinking variants. OEL achieves consistent improvements over successive iterations, enhancing both task accuracy and token efficiency while preserving out-of-distribution performance. Our analysis further shows that extracted experiential knowledge is significantly more effective than raw trajectories, and that on-policy consistency between the knowledge source and the policy model is critical for effective learning. 23. Anticipatory Planning for Multimodal AI Agents

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16777v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Recent advances in multimodal agents have improved computer-use interaction and tool-usage, yet most existing systems remain reactive, optimizing actions in isolation without reasoning about future states or long-term goals. This limits planning coherence and prevents agents from reliably solving high-level, multi-step tasks. We introduce TraceR1, a two-stage reinforcement learning framework that explicitly trains anticipatory reasoning by forecasting short-horizon trajectories before execution. The first stage performs trajectory-level reinforcement learning with rewards that enforce global consistency across predicted action sequences. The second stage applies grounded reinforcement fine-tuning, using execution feedback from frozen tool agents to refine step-level accuracy and executability. TraceR1 is evaluated across seven benchmarks, covering online computer-use, offline computer-use benchmarks, and multimodal tool-use reasoning tasks, where it achieves substantial improvements in planning stability, execution robustness, and generalization over reactive and single-stage baselines. These results show that anticipatory trajectory reasoning is a key principle for building multim
  • 易漏细节梳理：

反应系统在优化独立动作时通常不考虑未来状态，这可能导致局部优化而忽视全局一致性。为了解决这一问题，首先在第一个阶段通过强制执行全局一致性来确保动作序列的协调性。其次，在第二个阶段利用执行反馈来进一步提高步骤级别的准确性。TraceR1通过改进规划稳定性和执行鲁棒性，以及增强泛化能力，实现了这些目标。对于复杂的真实世界环境，前瞻性的轨迹推理至关重要，而单阶段基线方法则缺乏这种规划的连贯性。为了评估这些方法，使用了包括在线和离线基准在内的多种任务场景，以及多模态工具使用推理任务。大多数现有系统在规划连贯性方面都存在局限性，因此，通过强化学习训练前瞻性的推理能力，可以预测短期轨迹，从而增强执行效果。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • reactive systems optimize actions in isolation without considering future states.
  • global consistency across action sequences is enforced in the first stage.
  • execution feedback is used to refine step-level accuracy in the second stage.
  • TraceR1 improves planning stability, execution robustness, and generalization.
  • anticipatory trajectory reasoning is crucial for complex real-world environments.
  • single-stage baselines lack the planning coherence of TraceR1.
  • online and offline benchmarks cover various task scenarios.
  • multimodal tool-use reasoning tasks are included in the evaluation.
  • planning coherence is limited in most existing systems.
  • reinforcement learning is used to train anticipatory reasoning.
  • forecasting short-horizon trajectories enhances execution.

Rossi , Ruiyi Zhang View a PDF of the paper titled Anticipatory Planning for Multimodal AI Agents, by Yongyuan Liang and 8 other authors View PDF HTML (experimental) Abstract: Recent advances in multimodal agents have improved computer-use interaction and tool-usage, yet most existing systems remain reactive, optimizing actions in isolation without reasoning about future states or long-term goals. 24. Multi-Robot Decentralized Collaborative SLAM in Planetary Analogue Environments: Dataset, Challenges, and Lessons Learned

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.21063v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Decentralized collaborative simultaneous localization and mapping (C-SLAM) is essential to enable multirobot missions in unknown environments without relying on preexisting localization and communication infrastructure. This technology is anticipated to play a key role in the exploration of the Moon, Mars, and other planets. In this article, we share insights and lessons learned from C-SLAM experiments involving three robots operating on a Mars analogue terrain and communicating over an ad hoc network. We examine the impact of limited and intermittent communication on C-SLAM performance, as well as the unique localization challenges posed by planetary-like environments. Additionally, we introduce a novel dataset collected during our experiments, which includes real-time peer-to-peer inter-robot throughput and latency measurements. This dataset aims to support future research on communication-constrained, decentralized multirobot operations.
  • 易漏细节梳理：

ad hoc网络可能导致通信受限和间歇性通信，这在行星探索中尤为关键，尤其是在月球、火星及其他行星的探索中，C-SLAM技术对于这些环境下的探索至关重要。然而，行星环境下的独特定位挑战会影响C-SLAM性能，因此，实时的peer-to-peer通信吞吐量和延迟测量对于研究至关重要，这有助于克服定位挑战并提升C-SLAM技术的性能。因此，通过实时监测通信质量，可以更好地应对ad hoc网络带来的通信限制，从而确保在复杂行星环境中的有效通信和探索。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • ad hoc网络可能导致通信受限和间歇性通信。
  • 行星环境下的独特定位挑战会影响C-SLAM性能。
  • 实时的 peer-to-peer 通信吞吐量和延迟测量对于研究至关重要。
  • C-SLAM技术对于月球、火星及其他行星的探索至关重要。

25. Fine-Grained Network Traffic Classification with Contextual QoS Profiling

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16748v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Accurate network traffic classification is vital for managing modern applications with strict Quality of Service (QoS) demands, such as edge computing, real-time XR, and autonomous systems. While recent advances in application-level classification show high accuracy, they often miss fine-grained in-app QoS variations critical for service differentiation. This paper proposes a hierarchical graph neural network (GNN) framework that combines a three-level graph representation with an automated QoS-aware assignment algorithm. The model captures multi-scale temporal patterns via packet aggregation, time-window clustering, and session-level behavior modeling. QoS priorities are derived using five key metrics (bandwidth, jitter, packet stability, burst frequency, and burst stability), processed through logarithmic transformation and weighted ranking. Evaluations across 14 usage scenarios from YouTube, Prime Video, TikTok, and Zoom show that the proposed GNN significantly outperforms state-of-the-art methods in service-level classification. The QoS-aware assignment further refines classification to enhance user experience. This work advances QoS-aware traffic classification by enabling pre

[2603.16748v1] Fine-Grained Network Traffic Classification with Contextual QoS Profiling Computer Science > Networking and Internet Architecture arXiv:2603.16748v1 (cs) [Submitted on 17 Mar 2026] Title: Fine-Grained Network Traffic Classification with Contextual QoS Profiling Authors: Huiwen Zhang , Feng Ye View a PDF of the paper titled Fine-Grained Network Traffic Classification with Contextual QoS Profiling, by Huiwen Zhang and 1 other authors View PDF HTML (experimental) Abstract: Accurate network traffic classification is vital for managing modern applications with strict Quality of Service (QoS) demands, such as edge computing, real-time XR, and autonomous systems. While recent advances in application-level classification show high accuracy, they often miss fine-grained in-app QoS variations critical for service differentiation. This paper proposes a hierarchical graph neural network (GNN) framework that combines a three-level graph representation with an automated QoS-aware assignment algorithm. The QoS-aware assignment further refines classification to enhance user experience. This work advances QoS-aware traffic classification by enabling precise in-app usage differentiation and adaptive service prioritization in dynamic network environments. 26. A Variational Pseudo-Observation Guided Nudged Particle Filter

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16705v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Nonlinear filtering with standard PF methods requires mitigative techniques to quell weight degeneracy, such as resampling. This is especially true in high-dimensional systems with sparse observations. Unfortunately, such techniques are also fragile when applied to systems with exceedingly rare events. Nonlinear systems with these properties can be assimilated effectively with a control-based PF method known as the nPF, but this method has a high computational cost burden. In this work, we aim to retain this strength of the nudged method while reducing the computational cost by introducing a variational method into the algorithm that acts as a continuous pseudo-observation path. By maintaining a PF representation, the resulting algorithm continues to capture an approximation of the filtering distribution, while reducing computational runtime and improving robustness to the "rare" event of switching phases. Preliminary testing of the new approach is demonstrated on a stochastic variant of the nonlinear and chaotic L63 model, which is used as a surrogate for mimicking "rare" events. The new approach helps to overcome difficulties in applying the nPF for realistic problems and perform
  • 易漏细节梳理：

weight degeneracy需要通过重采样等技术来缓解，但这些技术在高维系统和稀疏观测下特别脆弱。稀疏观测和高维系统的非线性过滤尤其需要控制基于粒子滤波的方法，但这种方法计算成本高。为了解决这一问题，引入变分方法可以降低计算成本，同时保持粒子滤波的表示。新方法在处理真实问题时能有效克服nPF的困难，并优于标准粒子滤波。稀有事件的切换相态对计算稳健性有重大影响，因此L63模型的随机变体被用作模拟稀有事件的代理。新方法不仅在计算时间和鲁棒性方面表现出优势，还能更有效地处理稀疏观测和高维系统中的非线性过滤问题。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • weight degeneracy需要通过重采样等技术来缓解，但这些技术在高维系统和稀疏观测下特别脆弱。
  • 稀疏观测和高维系统的非线性过滤尤其需要控制基于粒子滤波的方法，但这种方法计算成本高。
  • 引入变分方法可以降低计算成本，同时保持粒子滤波的表示。
  • 新方法在处理真实问题时能有效克服nPF的困难，并优于标准粒子滤波。
  • 稀有事件的切换相态对计算稳健性有重大影响。
  • L63模型的随机变体被用作模拟稀有事件的代理。
  • 新方法在计算时间和鲁棒性方面表现出优势。

27. M^3: Dense Matching Meets Multi-View Foundation Models for Monocular Gaussian Splatting SLAM

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16844v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Streaming reconstruction from uncalibrated monocular video remains challenging, as it requires both high-precision pose estimation and computationally efficient online refinement in dynamic environments. While coupling 3D foundation models with SLAM frameworks is a promising paradigm, a critical bottleneck persists: most multi-view foundation models estimate poses in a feed-forward manner, yielding pixel-level correspondences that lack the requisite precision for rigorous geometric optimization. To address this, we present M^3, which augments the Multi-view foundation model with a dedicated Matching head to facilitate fine-grained dense correspondences and integrates it into a robust Monocular Gaussian Splatting SLAM. M^3 further enhances tracking stability by incorporating dynamic area suppression and cross-inference intrinsic alignment. Extensive experiments on diverse indoor and outdoor benchmarks demonstrate state-of-the-art accuracy in both pose estimation and scene reconstruction. Notably, M^3 reduces ATE RMSE by 64.3% compared to VGGT-SLAM 2.0 and outperforms ARTDECO by 2.11 dB in PSNR on the ScanNet++ dataset.
  • 易漏细节梳理：

首先，feed-forward估计方式由于缺乏必要的精度，导致了跟踪过程中可能出现的误差。为解决这一问题，M^3引入了专门的匹配头，以提高精度，从而使得跟踪结果更加可靠。此外，动态区域抑制技术的应用有助于提高跟踪的稳定性，通过抑制不必要的区域，使得跟踪更加专注于关键区域，从而减少干扰。进一步地，跨推断内联对齐技术的应用增强了整体的稳定性，通过更紧密的对齐，确保了不同帧之间的连续性和一致性。因此，M^3在多种室内和室外基准上表现出色，特别是在ATE RMSE上比VGGT-SLAM 2.0降低了64.3%，在PSNR上比ARTDECO提高了2.11 dB。然而，未校准的单目视频流式重建仍然具有挑战性，这表明尽管M^3在多视图基础模型中以像素级对应关系进行估计，但单目视频的校准问题仍然是一个需要解决的难题。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • feed-forward估计方式缺乏必要的精度。
  • M^3增加了专门的匹配头以提高精度。
  • 动态区域抑制有助于提高跟踪稳定性。
  • 跨推断内联对齐进一步增强了稳定性。
  • M^3在ATE RMSE上比VGGT-SLAM 2.0降低了64.3%。
  • M^3在PSNR上比ARTDECO提高了2.11 dB。
  • 多视图基础模型通常以像素级对应关系进行估计。
  • M^3在多种室内和室外基准上表现出色。
  • 未校准的单目视频流式重建仍具有挑战性。

28. Mediocrity is the key for LLM as a Judge Anchor Selection

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16848v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：The ``LLM-as-a-judge'' paradigm has become a standard method for evaluating open-ended generation. To address the quadratic scalability costs of pairwise comparisons, popular benchmarks like Arena-Hard and AlpacaEval compare all models against a single anchor. However, despite its widespread use, the impact of anchor selection on the reliability of the results remains largely unexplored. In this work, we systematically investigate the effect of anchor selection by evaluating 22 different anchors on the Arena-Hard-v2.0 dataset. We find that the choice of anchor is critical: a poor anchor can dramatically reduce correlation with human rankings. We identify that common anchor choices (best-performing and worst-performing models) make poor anchors. Because these extreme anchors are consistently better or worse than all other models, they are seldom indicative of the relative ranking of the models. We further quantify the effect size of anchor selection, showing it is comparable to the selection of a judge model. We conclude with actionable recommendations. First, we conduct a power analysis, and compute sufficient benchmark sizes for anchor-based evaluation, finding that standard bench
  • 易漏细节梳理：

首先，锚点的选择对结果的可靠性有着显著的影响。合适的锚点能够提供一个准确的参照，从而提高评价的准确性。其次，极端模型作为锚点的效果并不理想，因为它们往往过于简化或复杂，无法准确反映实际情况。此外，标准基准的大小通常不足以进行两两比较，因为它们可能过于宽泛，无法提供足够的细节。因此，选择合适的锚点对评价至关重要，其影响甚至可以与选择评判模型相提并论。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • anchor选择对结果可靠性影响显著。
  • 极端模型作为锚点效果不佳。
  • 标准基准大小不足以进行两两比较。
  • 选择合适的锚点对评价至关重要。
  • 锚点选择的影响与选择评判模型相当。

[2603.16848v1] Mediocrity is the key for LLM as a Judge Anchor Selection Computer Science > Computation and Language arXiv:2603.16848v1 (cs) [Submitted on 17 Mar 2026] Title: Mediocrity is the key for LLM as a Judge Anchor Selection Authors: Shachar Don-Yehiya , Asaf Yehudai , Leshem Choshen , Omri Abend View a PDF of the paper titled Mediocrity is the key for LLM as a Judge Anchor Selection, by Shachar Don-Yehiya and 3 other authors View PDF HTML (experimental) Abstract: The ``LLM-as-a-judge'' paradigm has become a standard method for evaluating open-ended generation. To address the quadratic scalability costs of pairwise comparisons, popular benchmarks like Arena-Hard and AlpacaEval compare all models against a single anchor. However, despite its widespread use, the impact of anchor selection on the reliability of the results remains largely unexplored. In this work, we systematically investigate the effect of anchor selection by evaluating 22 different anchors on the Arena-Hard-v2.0 dataset. We find that the choice of anchor is critical: a poor anchor can dramatically reduce correlation with human rankings. First, we conduct a power analysis, and compute sufficient benchmark sizes for anchor-based evaluation, finding that standard benchmark sizes are insufficient for pairwise evaluation and fail to distinguish between competitive models reliably. Second, we provide guidelines for selecting informative anchors to ensure reliable and efficient evaluation practices. 29. SegviGen: Repurposing 3D Generative Model for Part Segmentation

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16869v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：We introduce SegviGen, a framework that repurposes native 3D generative models for 3D part segmentation. Existing pipelines either lift strong 2D priors into 3D via distillation or multi-view mask aggregation, often suffering from cross-view inconsistency and blurred boundaries, or explore native 3D discriminative segmentation, which typically requires large-scale annotated 3D data and substantial training resources. In contrast, SegviGen leverages the structured priors encoded in pretrained 3D generative model to induce segmentation through distinctive part colorization, establishing a novel and efficient framework for part segmentation. Specifically, SegviGen encodes a 3D asset and predicts part-indicative colors on active voxels of a geometry-aligned reconstruction. It supports interactive part segmentation, full segmentation, and full segmentation with 2D guidance in a unified framework. Extensive experiments show that SegviGen improves over the prior state of the art by 40% on interactive part segmentation and by 15% on full segmentation, while using only 0.32% of the labeled training data. It demonstrates that pretrained 3D generative priors transfer effectively to 3D part se
  • 易漏细节梳理：

首先，D priors在提升到3D时常常会面临跨视角不一致的问题，这可能导致边界模糊。其次，SegviGen通过使用预训练的3D生成模型的结构化先验，有效地解决了这一问题。此外，SegviGen支持交互式、完整和引导式完整部分分割，显著提升了交互式部分分割的性能，相较于之前的方法，提高了40%。同时，它也提升了完整分割的性能，相比之前的方法提高了15%。值得注意的是，SegviGen仅使用了0.32%的标注训练数据，这表明它能够利用有限的监督实现强大的性能。因此，预训练的3D生成模型先验能够有效地转移到3D部分分割任务中，即使监督有限，也能取得优异的结果。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • D priors often suffer from cross-view inconsistency when lifted into 3D.
  • Multi-view mask aggregation can lead to blurred boundaries.
  • Native 3D discriminative segmentation requires large-scale annotated data.
  • SegviGen uses structured priors from pretrained 3D generative models.
  • SegviGen supports interactive, full, and guided full part segmentation.
  • SegviGen improves interactive part segmentation by 40% over previous methods.
  • SegviGen improves full segmentation by 15% over previous methods.
  • SegviGen uses only 0.32% of the labeled training data.
  • Pretrained 3D generative priors can effectively transfer to 3D part segmentation.
  • Limited supervision can still achieve strong performance with SegviGen.

[2603.16869v1] SegviGen: Repurposing 3D Generative Model for Part Segmentation Computer Science > Computer Vision and Pattern Recognition arXiv:2603.16869v1 (cs) [Submitted on 17 Mar 2026] Title: SegviGen: Repurposing 3D Generative Model for Part Segmentation Authors: Lin Li , Haoran Feng , Zehuan Huang , Haohua Chen , Wenbo Nie , Shaohua Hou , Keqing Fan , Pan Hu , Sheng Wang , Buyu Li , Lu Sheng View a PDF of the paper titled SegviGen: Repurposing 3D Generative Model for Part Segmentation, by Lin Li and 10 other authors View PDF HTML (experimental) Abstract: We introduce SegviGen, a framework that repurposes native 3D generative models for 3D part segmentation. Existing pipelines either lift strong 2D priors into 3D via distillation or multi-view mask aggregation, often suffering from cross-view inconsistency and blurred boundaries, or explore native 3D discriminative segmentation, which typically requires large-scale annotated 3D data and substantial training resources. In contrast, SegviGen leverages the structured priors encoded in pretrained 3D generative model to induce segmentation through distinctive part colorization, establishing a novel and efficient framework for part segmentation. Specifically, SegviGen encodes a 3D asset and predicts part-indicative colors on active voxels of a geometry-aligned reconstruction. It supports interactive part segmentation, full segmentation, and full segmentation with 2D guidance in a unified framework. Extensive experiments show that SegviGen improves over the prior state of the art by 40% on interactive part segmentation and by 15% on full segmentation, while using only 0.32% of the labeled training data. It demonstrates that pretrained 3D generative priors transfer effectively to 3D part segmentation, enabling strong performance with limited supervision. See our project page at this https URL . 30. ManiTwin: Scaling Data-Generation-Ready Digital Object Dataset to 100K

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16866v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Learning in simulation provides a useful foundation for scaling robotic manipulation capabilities. However, this paradigm often suffers from a lack of data-generation-ready digital assets, in both scale and diversity. In this work, we present ManiTwin, an automated and efficient pipeline for generating data-generation-ready digital object twins. Our pipeline transforms a single image into simulation-ready and semantically annotated 3D asset, enabling large-scale robotic manipulation data generation. Using this pipeline, we construct ManiTwin-100K, a dataset containing 100K high-quality annotated 3D assets. Each asset is equipped with physical properties, language descriptions, functional annotations, and verified manipulation proposals. Experiments demonstrate that ManiTwin provides an efficient asset synthesis and annotation workflow, and that ManiTwin-100K offers high-quality and diverse assets for manipulation data generation, random scene synthesis, and VQA data generation, establishing a strong foundation for scalable simulation data synthesis and policy learning. Our webpage is available at https://manitwin.github.io/.
  • 易漏细节梳理：

ManiTwin 提供了高效的数据生成流程，生成的数字对象不仅具有物理属性和语言描述，还附带有功能注释，确保了数据的全面性和实用性。ManiTwin-100K 数据集包含100,000个高质量的3D资产，每个资产都附带验证过的操作提案，确保了数据的准确性和可靠性。合成和标注资产的工作流程高效且系统化，使得ManiTwin-100K不仅适用于操作数据生成，还能够支持随机场景合成和VQA数据生成。因此，ManiTwin-100K 为可扩展的模拟数据合成和策略学习奠定了基础，生成的3D资产经过语义标注，适用于大规模机器人操作数据生成，从而提升了模拟准备的效率和质量。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • ManiTwin 提供了高效的数据生成流程。
  • 生成的数字对象具有物理属性、语言描述和功能注释。
  • ManiTwin-100K 数据集包含 100,000 个高质量的 3D 资产。
  • 每个资产都附带验证过的操作提案。
  • 合成和标注资产的工作流程是高效的。
  • ManiTwin-100K 提供了高质量和多样化的资产，适用于操作数据生成。
  • ManiTwin-100K 适用于随机场景合成和 VQA 数据生成。
  • ManiTwin 为可扩展的模拟数据合成和策略学习奠定了基础。
  • 生成的 3D 资产是模拟准备的。
  • 每个 3D 资产都经过语义标注。
  • 生成的数字对象可以用于大规模机器人操作数据生成。

31. InCoder-32B: Code Foundation Model for Industrial Scenarios

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16790v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Recent code large language models have achieved remarkable progress on general programming tasks. Nevertheless, their performance degrades significantly in industrial scenarios that require reasoning about hardware semantics, specialized language constructs, and strict resource constraints. To address these challenges, we introduce InCoder-32B (Industrial-Coder-32B), the first 32B-parameter code foundation model unifying code intelligence across chip design, GPU kernel optimization, embedded systems, compiler optimization, and 3D modeling. By adopting an efficient architecture, we train InCoder-32B from scratch with general code pre-training, curated industrial code annealing, mid-training that progressively extends context from 8K to 128K tokens with synthetic industrial reasoning data, and post-training with execution-grounded verification. We conduct extensive evaluation on 14 mainstream general code benchmarks and 9 industrial benchmarks spanning 4 specialized domains. Results show InCoder-32B achieves highly competitive performance on general tasks while establishing strong open-source baselines across industrial domains.
  • 易漏细节梳理：

InCoder-32B在训练过程中使用了从8K到128K不等的上下文长度，并通过合成工业推理数据逐步扩展上下文长度，这使得模型在工业场景中的表现优于通用编程任务。此外，InCoder-32B在多个工业基准测试中建立了强大的开源基线，并首次实现了统一芯片设计、GPU内核优化等领域的代码智能。其训练过程包括一般代码预训练和专门的工业代码调整，采用了高效的架构，并通过执行验证进行后训练。因此，InCoder-32B在14个主流通用代码基准和9个工业基准上进行了广泛评估，展示了其在工业领域的强大应用潜力。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • InCoder-32B的训练过程中使用了从8K到128K不等的上下文长度。
  • InCoder-32B通过合成工业推理数据来逐步扩展上下文长度。
  • InCoder-32B在工业场景中的表现优于通用编程任务。
  • InCoder-32B在多个工业基准测试中建立了强大的开源基线。
  • InCoder-32B首次实现了统一芯片设计、GPU内核优化等领域的代码智能。
  • InCoder-32B的训练包括一般代码预训练和专门的工业代码调整。
  • InCoder-32B的训练采用了高效的架构。
  • InCoder-32B通过执行验证进行后训练。
  • InCoder-32B在14个主流通用代码基准和9个工业基准上进行了广泛评估。

32. Measurement-Based Estimation of Causal Conditional Variances and Its Application to Macroscopic quantum phenomenon

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16821v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：We analytically investigate a quantum estimation method for a mechanical oscillator in a detuned cavity system based solely on homodyne measurement records, building on the framework developed by C.Meng et al. (Science Advances 8, 7585 (2022)). Estimation based only on measurement records is important because it enables state verification without assuming knowledge of the true system state. We construct a relative estimate operator from causal and anti-causal quantum Wiener filters and calculate its variance. The deviation from the causal conditional variance is defined as a reconstruction bias, whose magnitude is evaluated analytically. We show that, within experimentally relevant parameter regimes for typical quantum-state preparation, the reconstruction bias is sufficiently small to be neglected. As applications to state verification, we apply the method to proposals for macroscopic quantum entanglement mediated by electromagnetic interactions and for conditional momentum-squeezed states generated by homodyne detection, and clarify the conditions under which the bias remains negligible and when the reconstruction bias becomes significant.
  • 易漏细节梳理：

状态验证不需要知道真实的系统状态，而是通过量子Wiener滤波器来构建估计算子，其中因果和反因果量子Wiener滤波器被用于这一过程。具体而言，量子Wiener滤波器利用同调测量记录来实现量子状态的估计，而这种估计依赖于同调测量记录的可用性。在实验相关的参数范围内，重建偏差可以忽略不计，这意味着在这些条件下，状态验证的结果较为可靠。然而，在某些条件下，重建偏差变得显著，这表明在这些条件下需要更加精确的测量和分析。此外，这种方法适用于调谐腔系统，其中宏观量子纠缠和条件动量压缩态都可以通过这种方法进行验证。因此，状态验证的关键在于测量记录的同调性，而重建偏差的可忽略性则取决于具体的实验条件。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • state verification does not require knowledge of the true system state.
  • reconstruction bias measures the deviation from causal conditional variance.
  • causal and anti-causal quantum Wiener filters are used to construct the estimate operator.
  • homodyne measurement records enable quantum state estimation.
  • reconstruction bias is negligible in experimentally relevant parameter regimes.
  • macroscopic quantum entanglement can be verified using this method.
  • conditional momentum-squeezed states can also be verified using this method.
  • the bias becomes significant under certain conditions.
  • the method applies to detuned cavity systems.
  • homogeneous measurement records are sufficient for state verification.

33. A Jacobi Field Approach to Splitting Detection in Schrödinger Bridge

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16618v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：We study the problem of detecting the onset of path splitting in stochastic interpolation between probability distributions. This question is especially subtle when the target distribution is nonconvex or supported on disconnected components, where interpolating trajectories may separate into distinct branches. Motivated by the stochastic control and Schrödinger bridge viewpoint, we propose a Jacobi field based indicator for identifying candidate splitting times and locations. Our approach is based on the Jacobi field associated with the linearization of an induced interpolating flow. Starting from a stochastic interpolation ansatz, we construct an Eulerian velocity field by conditional averaging and derive its spatial Jacobian in terms of the local posterior geometry of the target sample cloud. This allows us to interpret the symmetric part of the Jacobian as a local strain tensor and to use its spectral structure to quantify the amplification of infinitesimal perturbations along reference trajectories. Numerical experiments on non-convex and disconnected target distributions show that the proposed indicator consistently localizes the emergence of branching regions and captures th
  • 易漏细节梳理：

非凸或支持在断连组件上的目标分布使得路径分离特别难以检测，这主要是因为这些特性使得路径分离的检测更加复杂。路径分离的检测涉及对目标样本云的局部后验几何的理解，而Eulerian速度场则是通过条件平均构建的。谱结构用于量化沿参考轨迹的无穷小扰动的放大，这反映了局部后验几何的物理意义。数值实验表明，所提出的方法能够一致地定位分支区域的出现，这进一步证实了路径分离检测的有效性。路径分离的检测依赖于诱导插值流的线性化，而Jacobi场分析则提供了一个自然的数学框架来研究随机插值中的局部不稳定性。因此，Jacobi场分析不仅能够提供一种研究随机插值中局部不稳定性的方法，还能够帮助理解路径分离检测的原理。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • 非凸或支持在断连组件上的目标分布使得路径分离特别难以检测。
  • 路径分离的检测涉及对目标样本云的局部后验几何的理解。
  • Eulerian速度场通过条件平均构建。
  • 谱结构用于量化沿参考轨迹的无穷小扰动的放大。
  • 数值实验表明，所提出的方法能够一致地定位分支区域的出现。
  • Jacobi场分析提供了一个自然的数学框架来研究随机插值中的局部不稳定性。
  • 目标分布的非凸性或断连性使得路径分离的检测更加复杂。
  • 路径分离的检测依赖于诱导插值流的线性化。
  • 局部后验几何解释了谱结构的物理意义。
  • 路径分离的检测方法基于Jacobi场。
  • Jacobi场分析提供了一种研究随机插值中局部不稳定性的方法。

[2603.16618v1] A Jacobi Field Approach to Splitting Detection in Schrödinger Bridge Mathematics > Dynamical Systems arXiv:2603.16618v1 (math) [Submitted on 17 Mar 2026] Title: A Jacobi Field Approach to Splitting Detection in Schrödinger Bridge Authors: Chunhai Jiao , Jin Guo , Haoyan Zhang , Jinqiao Duan , Ting Gao View a PDF of the paper titled A Jacobi Field Approach to Splitting Detection in Schr\"{o}dinger Bridge, by Chunhai Jiao and 4 other authors View PDF HTML (experimental) Abstract: We study the problem of detecting the onset of path splitting in stochastic interpolation between probability distributions. This question is especially subtle when the target distribution is nonconvex or supported on disconnected components, where interpolating trajectories may separate into distinct branches. Motivated by the stochastic control and Schrödinger bridge viewpoint, we propose a Jacobi field based indicator for identifying candidate splitting times and locations. Our approach is based on the Jacobi field associated with the linearization of an induced interpolating flow. Starting from a stochastic interpolation ansatz, we construct an Eulerian velocity field by conditional averaging and derive its spatial Jacobian in terms of the local posterior geometry of the target sample cloud. This allows us to interpret the symmetric part of the Jacobian as a local strain tensor and to use its spectral structure to quantify the amplification of infinitesimal perturbations along reference trajectories. Numerical experiments on non-convex and disconnected target distributions show that the proposed indicator consistently localizes the emergence of branching regions and captures the temporal development of splitting. These results suggest that Jacobi field analysis provides a natural mathematical framework for studying local instability and splitting phenomena in stochastic interpolation. 34. Quantum-Enabled Probabilistic Optimal Power Flow with Built-in Differential Privacy

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16780v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Quantum computing has been regarded as a promising approach to accelerate power system optimization. However, challenges such as limited qubits and inherent noise hinder their widespread adoption in power systems. In this paper, we propose a qubit-efficient framework for solving a crucial power system optimization problem, the probabilistic optimal power flow (POPF). We demonstrate that quantum noise, traditionally viewed as a drawback, can in fact be leveraged to provide a built-in differential privacy (DP) guarantee. Specifically, we first linearize POPF into a multi-parametric linear program (MP-LP) with renewable uncertainties being the parameters. This decomposes the parameter space into critical regions with precomputed solution maps. Second, a variational quantum circuit (VQC) classifies the critical region based on each uncertainty realization and then recovers the final solution. In this way, the required qubits scale with the uncertain parameters instead of the network size, with only 5 qubits versus 600+ for direct quantum OPF in a 69-bus system. Moreover, we prove the depolarizing noise of VQC provides DP guarantees and characterize the privacy-cost tradeoff. Case studi
  • 易漏细节梳理：

首先，量子噪声通常被视为量子计算中的一个缺点，但本文展示了它可以被利用来提供差分隐私保证。具体而言，量子变分量子本征态算法（VQC）的去极化噪声可以提供差分隐私，同时在匹配隐私水平下保持更低的不可行性和预测误差。其次，参数空间被分解成关键区域，每个区域都有预先计算的解图，这有助于优化算法的性能。此外，VQC的qubit需求与不确定参数成比例，而不是网络规模，使得其在资源上更加高效。案例研究进一步验证了VQC的优越性，结果显示VQC在69-节点系统中仅需5个qubit，而直接量子最优潮流（OPF）则需要600多个qubit。因此，尽管差分隐私成本与经典方法相比有所权衡，VQC仍能实现2.1倍较小的隐私预算，展示了其在实际应用中的潜力。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • 量子噪声可以被利用来提供内置的差分隐私保证。
  • 参数空间被分解成关键区域，每个区域都有预先计算的解图。
  • VQC的去极化噪声提供差分隐私保证。
  • VQC在匹配隐私水平下保持更低的不可行性和预测误差。
  • 传统上认为量子噪声是缺点，但本文展示了它可以被利用来提供差分隐私。
  • VQC的qubit需求与不确定参数成比例，而不是网络规模。
  • 直接量子OPF在69-节点系统中需要600多个qubit，而VQC仅需5个。
  • 差分隐私成本与经典方法相比有所权衡。
  • 案例研究验证了VQC实现了2.1倍较小的隐私预算。

[2603.16780v1] Quantum-Enabled Probabilistic Optimal Power Flow with Built-in Differential Privacy Mathematics > Optimization and Control arXiv:2603.16780v1 (math) [Submitted on 17 Mar 2026] Title: Quantum-Enabled Probabilistic Optimal Power Flow with Built-in Differential Privacy Authors: Yuji Cao , Tongxin Li , Yue Chen View a PDF of the paper titled Quantum-Enabled Probabilistic Optimal Power Flow with Built-in Differential Privacy, by Yuji Cao and 2 other authors View PDF HTML (experimental) Abstract: Quantum computing has been regarded as a promising approach to accelerate power system optimization. However, challenges such as limited qubits and inherent noise hinder their widespread adoption in power systems. In this paper, we propose a qubit-efficient framework for solving a crucial power system optimization problem, the probabilistic optimal power flow (POPF). We demonstrate that quantum noise, traditionally viewed as a drawback, can in fact be leveraged to provide a built-in differential privacy (DP) guarantee. Specifically, we first linearize POPF into a multi-parametric linear program (MP-LP) with renewable uncertainties being the parameters. This decomposes the parameter space into critical regions with precomputed solution maps. Second, a variational quantum circuit (VQC) classifies the critical region based on each uncertainty realization and then recovers the final solution. In this way, the required qubits scale with the uncertain parameters instead of the network size, with only 5 qubits versus 600+ for direct quantum OPF in a 69-bus system. Moreover, we prove the depolarizing noise of VQC provides DP guarantees and characterize the privacy-cost tradeoff. Case studies validate the proposed VQC achieves 2.1$\times$ smaller privacy budgets compared to its classical counterpart. At matched privacy levels, the VQC also maintains lower infeasibility and prediction error. 35. SOMA: Unifying Parametric Human Body Models

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16858v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Parametric human body models are foundational to human reconstruction, animation, and simulation, yet they remain mutually incompatible: SMPL, SMPL-X, MHR, Anny, and related models each diverge in mesh topology, skeletal structure, shape parameterization, and unit convention, making it impractical to exploit their complementary strengths within a single pipeline. We present SOMA, a unified body layer that bridges these heterogeneous representations through three abstraction layers. Mesh topology abstraction maps any source model's identity to a shared canonical mesh in constant time per vertex. Skeletal abstraction recovers a full set of identity-adapted joint transforms from any body shape, whether in rest pose or an arbitrary posed configuration, in a single closed-form pass, with no iterative optimization or per-model training. Pose abstraction inverts the skinning pipeline to recover unified skeleton rotations directly from posed vertices of any supported model, enabling heterogeneous motion datasets to be consumed without custom retargeting. Together, these layers reduce the $O(M^2)$ per-pair adapter problem to $O(M)$ single-backend connectors, letting practitioners freely mix
  • 易漏细节梳理：

SOMA的每个抽象层都显著减少了计算复杂度，从而解决了不同人体模型之间的互不兼容问题。首先，Mesh拓扑抽象层能在常数时间内将任何源模型映射到共享的规范网格，这一步骤将每对适配器问题的复杂度从O(M^2)降低到O(M)。其次，骨骼抽象层能一次性恢复任何体型的完整关节变换，进一步简化了计算过程。此外，姿势抽象层能直接从任何支持模型的变形顶点中恢复统一的骨架旋转，确保了整个管道的端到端可微分性并使用NVIDIA-Warp进行GPU加速。因此，这些层共同作用，使得不同的身份源和姿势数据可以在推理时自由混合，从而大幅提高了处理不同人体模型适配问题的效率和灵活性。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • SOMA的每个抽象层都显著减少了计算复杂度。
  • Mesh拓扑抽象层能在常数时间内将任何源模型映射到共享的规范网格。
  • 骨骼抽象层能一次性恢复任何体型的完整关节变换。
  • 姿势抽象层能直接从任何支持模型的变形顶点中恢复统一的骨架旋转。
  • 这些层共同将每对适配器问题的复杂度从O(M^2)降低到O(M)。
  • 整个管道是端到端可微分并使用NVIDIA-Warp进行GPU加速。
  • 不同的身份源和姿势数据可以在推理时自由混合。
  • SOMA解决了不同人体模型之间的互不兼容问题。
  • 每个抽象层都减少了不同人体模型之间的适配问题。

36. Internalizing Agency from Reflective Experience

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16843v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Large language models are increasingly deployed as autonomous agents that must plan, act, and recover from mistakes through long-horizon interaction with environments that provide rich feedback. However, prevailing outcome-driven post-training methods (e.g., RL with verifiable rewards) primarily optimize final success signals, leaving rich environment feedback underutilized. Consequently, they often lead to distribution sharpening: the policy becomes better at reproducing a narrow set of already-successful behaviors, while failing to improve the feedback-grounded agency needed to expand problem-solving capacity (e.g., Pass@k) in long-horizon settings. To address this, we propose LEAFE (Learning Feedback-Grounded Agency from Reflective Experience), a framework that internalizes recovery agency from reflective experience. Specifically, during exploration, the agent summarizes environment feedback into actionable experience, backtracks to earlier decision points, and explores alternative branches with revised actions. We then distill these experience-guided corrections into the model through supervised fine-tuning, enabling the policy to recover more effectively in future interactio
  • 易漏细节梳理：

LEAFE框架利用反思经验来提升代理的恢复能力，通过总结环境反馈为可操作的经验，以指导代理的恢复。这种反馈驱动的代理能力对于长期交互至关重要，有助于扩展问题解决能力。相比之下，先前的方法主要优化最终的成功信号，忽视了丰富的环境反馈。LEAFE通过监督微调将经验指导的修正注入模型，从而在多种交互任务中显著提高了Pass@1和Pass@k指标。具体而言，LEAFE在Pass@128上取得了高达14%的改进，这进一步证明了其在长期交互中的优越性。因此，LEAFE不仅提升了代理的恢复能力，还显著增强了其在复杂任务中的表现。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • LEAFE框架利用反思经验来提升代理的恢复能力。
  • 环境反馈被总结为可操作的经验，以指导代理的恢复。
  • 反馈驱动的代理能力对于长期交互至关重要。
  • LEAFE在多种交互任务中提高了Pass@1和Pass@k指标。
  • 先前的方法主要优化最终的成功信号，忽视了丰富的环境反馈。
  • 反馈驱动的代理能力有助于扩展问题解决能力。
  • LEAFE通过监督微调将经验指导的修正注入模型。
  • Pass@k衡量了长期交互中的问题解决能力。
  • LEAFE在Pass@128上取得了高达14%的改进。
